class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph" style="border-style:none;border-width:0px;font-size:25px">Raw feeding isn&rsquo;t about perfection or rigid rules. It&rsquo;s about nourishing your dog with real food that supports digestion, skin, energy, and long-term health &mdash; while still fitting into everyday life with dogs.</p><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph" style="border-style:none;border-width:0px;font-size:25px">On K9sOverCoffee, you&rsquo;ll find practical raw dog food guidance alongside real-life dog lifestyle content, so you can feed your dog with confidence and still enjoy life together.</p><div class="wp-block-columns has-border-color has-black-border-color is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-075ea9ba wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="border-width:5px;border-top-left-radius:0px;border-top-right-radius:0px;border-bottom-left-radius:0px;border-bottom-right-radius:0px;margin-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--20);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--40);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--20);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--40)"><div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">New to Raw Feeding? Start Here</h2><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph"><strong>Raw feeding isn&rsquo;t about perfection &mdash; it&rsquo;s about feeding the dog in front of you.</strong><br>If you&rsquo;re new to raw dog food and feeling overwhelmed by ratios, rules, and conflicting advice, you&rsquo;re not alone.</p><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph">I&rsquo;ve been raw feeding since 2015 and created a beginner-friendly guide that focuses on clarity, confidence, and practical next steps &mdash; no fear tactics, no pressure to &ldquo;do it perfectly.&rdquo;</p><p class="has-text-align-center has-ast-global-color-2-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-7b26485a743e5d35ec9bd6c41a730024 wp-block-paragraph"><strong><a href="https://k9sovercoffee.com/quick-start-guide-to-raw-dog-food/" data-type="link" data-id="https://k9sovercoffee.com/quick-start-guide-to-raw-dog-food/">Start raw feeding with confidence &rarr;</a></strong></p></div><div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Raw Feeding for Dogs With Sensitivities</h2><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph"><strong>Itching, licking, ear issues, digestive upset &mdash; sound familiar?</strong><br>Many dogs with food sensitivities do better on fresh, species-appropriate diets, but raw feeding with allergies requires a thoughtful approach.</p><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph">On K9sOverCoffee, I share what&rsquo;s worked for my own dogs, including elimination diets, novel proteins, and how to build simple meals without triggering symptoms.</p><p class="has-text-align-center has-ast-global-color-2-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-7df98651613c51158bedb9485b0bdec1 wp-block-paragraph"><strong><a href="https://k9sovercoffee.com/top-3-reasons-for-dog-allergies-symptoms-and-how-to-cure-them/" data-type="post" data-id="669">Learn how you can help your allergic dog &rarr;</a></strong></p></div><div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow"><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Raising a Puppy on Raw Food</h2><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph"><strong>Feeding a puppy raw doesn&rsquo;t have to be complicated.</strong><br>I&rsquo;m raising my Labrador puppy Pepper on a raw diet and documenting the journey step by step &mdash; from first meals to growth spurts, feeding percentages, and real-life adjustments along the way.</p><p class="has-text-align-center wp-block-paragraph">If you&rsquo;re wondering how much to feed, what nutrients matter most during growth, or whether raw is safe for puppies, start here.</p><p class="has-text-align-center has-ast-global-color-2-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ee86463b4bb529be7dcdd0b44ee6fc48 wp-block-paragraph"><strong><a href="https://k9sovercoffee.com/raw-feeding-labrador-puppy/" data-type="post" data-id="152003">Follow Pepper&rsquo;s puppy raw feeding journey &rarr;</a></strong></p></div></div></div><p class="wp-block-paragraph"></p><h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center">Featured Raw Dog Food
